\h1Tableaux
The following are approximate tableaux for this ranking.  Outputs are derived simply by sorting the constraints by their ranking value, with no stochastic variation.
To diagnose variation, consult two things:
--The candidate frequencies (which are the generated frequencies, not the input frequencies).
--The probability that each constraint outranks the next one down, given directly after the constraint labels.

\h1Ranking Value to Ranking Probability Conversion
The computed ranking values imply the pairwise ranking probabilities given below.  In the table, the probability given is that of the constraint in the row headings outranking the constraint in the column headings.

\ts13
	*F3_B1	*F3..._B1	*F3_B2	*F3..._B2	*_B1F3	*_B1...F3	*_B2F3	*_B2...F3	Id(Bk)Syl1	*B2	*F3	Id(Bk)
*B1	0.501	0.501	0.501	0.501	0.501	0.501	0.501	0.501	>.999999	>.999999	>.999999	>.999999
*F3_B1	\sh	0.501	0.501	0.501	0.501	0.501	0.501	0.501	>.999999	>.999999	>.999999	>.999999
*F3..._B1	\sh	\sh	0.501	0.501	0.501	0.501	0.501	0.501	>.999999	>.999999	>.999999	>.999999
*F3_B2	\sh	\sh	\sh	0.501	0.501	0.501	0.501	0.501	>.999999	>.999999	>.999999	>.999999
*F3..._B2	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	0.501	0.501	0.501	0.501	>.999999	>.999999	>.999999	>.999999
*_B1F3	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	0.501	0.501	0.501	>.999999	>.999999	>.999999	>.999999
*_B1...F3	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	0.501	0.501	>.999999	>.999999	>.999999	>.999999
*_B2F3	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	0.501	>.999999	>.999999	>.999999	>.999999
*_B2...F3	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	>.999999	>.999999	>.999999	>.999999
Id(Bk)Syl1	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	0.928	>.999999	>.999999
*B2	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	\sh	0.999989	>.999999

\h1Active Constraints
A constraint is active if it causes the winning candidate to defeat a rival in at least one competition.

\ts2
Constraint	Status
*B1	Active
*F3_B1	Active
*F3..._B1	Active
*F3_B2	Active
*F3..._B2	Active
*_B1F3	Active
*_B1...F3	Active
*_B2F3	Active
*_B2...F3	Active
Id(Bk)Syl1	Active
*B2	Active
*F3	Active
